  </tbody>
  
  
</table>

</exercise>

    <tr>
      <th style="color: #333333; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-size: 100%; font-weight: normal; text-transform: inherit; vertical-align: middle; padding: 5px; margin: 10px; overflow-x: hidden; text-align: center;" rowspan="2" colspan="1">Study</th>
      <th style="color: #333333; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-size: 100%; font-weight: normal; text-transform: inherit; vertical-align: middle; padding: 5px; margin: 10px; overflow-x: hidden; text-align: center;" rowspan="2" colspan="1">Number of participants</th>
      <th style="color: #333333; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-size: 100%; font-weight: normal; text-transform: inherit; vertical-align: middle; padding: 5px; margin: 10px; overflow-x: hidden; text-align: center;" rowspan="2" colspan="1">Number of paired measurements</th>
      <th style="color: #333333; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-size: 100%; font-weight: normal; text-transform: inherit; vertical-align: middle; padding: 5px; margin: 10px; overflow-x: hidden; text-align: center;" rowspan="2" colspan="1">Mean bias</th>
      <th style="color: #333333; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-size: 100%; font-weight: normal; text-transform: inherit; vertical-align: middle; padding: 5px; margin: 10px; overflow-x: hidden; text-align: center;" rowspan="2" colspan="1">Lower 95% limit of agreement</th>

      <th style="color: #333333; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-size: 100%; font-weight: normal; text-transform: inherit; vertical-align: middle; padding: 5px; margin: 10px; overflow-x: hidden; text-align: center;" rowspan="2" colspan="1">Location of comparator thermometer</th>
      <th style="color: #333333; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-size: 100%; font-weight: normal; text-transform: inherit; vertical-align: middle; padding: 5px; margin: 10px; overflow-x: hidden; text-align: center;" rowspan="2" colspan="1">Multiple measures taken for each participant</th>
      <th style="color: #333333; background-color: #FFFFFF; font-size: 100%; font-weight: normal; text-transform: inherit; vertical-align: middle; padding: 5px; margin: 10px; overflow-x: hidden; text-align: center;" rowspan="2" colspan="1">Patient population</th>
